    为指令定义一个 controller ， <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">function controller($scope, $element, $attrs, $transclude) { ... }</code>
</dd>
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">name</span></dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
    指令的 controller 的名字，方便其它指令引用。
</dd>
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">require</span></dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
    要引用的其它指令 conroller 的名字， <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">?name</code> 忽略不存在的错误， <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">^name</code> 在父级查找。
</dd>
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">template</span></dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
    模板内容。
</dd>
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">templateUrl</span></dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
    从指定地址获取模板内容。
</dd>
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">replace</span></dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
    是否使用模板内容替换掉整个节点， <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">true</code> 替换整个节点， <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">false</code> 替换节点内容。
</dd>
</dl>


<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;a b&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
</pre></div>



<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> app <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> angular.module(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>, [], angular.noop);
  
  app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'a'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
    <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> func <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(element, attrs, link){
      console.log(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'a'</span>);
    }
  
    <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> func,
            priority<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00ffff">1</span>,
            restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'EA'</span>};
  });
  
  app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'b'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
    <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> func <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(element, attrs, link){
      console.log(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'b'</span>);
    }
  
    <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> func,
            priority<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00ffff">2</span>,
            <span style="color: #507080">//terminal: true,</span>
            restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'A'</span>};
  });
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
上面几个参数值都是比较简单且容易理想的。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
再看 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">scope</span> 这个参数：
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;div ng-controller=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"TestCtrl"</span>&gt;
    &lt;div a b&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
</pre></div>



<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"><span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 1</span>   <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> app <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> angular.module(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>, [], angular.noop);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 2</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 3</span>   app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'a'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 4</span>     <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> func <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(element, attrs, link){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 5</span>       <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(scope){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 6</span>         console.log(scope);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 7</span>       }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 8</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 9</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">10</span>     <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> func,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">11</span>             scope<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #90ee90">true</span>,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">12</span>             restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'A'</span>};
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">13</span>   });
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">14</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">15</span>   app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'b'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">16</span>     <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> func <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(element, attrs, link){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">17</span>       <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(scope){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">18</span>         console.log(scope);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">19</span>       }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">20</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">21</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">22</span>     <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> func,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">23</span>             restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'A'</span>};
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">24</span>   });
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">25</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">26</span>   app.controller(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'TestCtrl'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">27</span>     $scope.a <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'123'</span>;
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">28</span>     console.log($scope);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">29</span>   });
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
对于 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">scope</span> ：
</p>

<ul style="line-height: 1.4em; padding-left: 20px; margin: auto 30px;">
<li>默认为 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">false</code> ， <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">link</code> 函数接受的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope</code> 为节点所在的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope</code> 。
</li>
<li>为 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">true</code> 时，则 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">link</code> 函数中第一个参数（还有 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">controller</code> 参数中的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">$scope</code> ）， <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope</code> 是节点所在的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope</code> 的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">child scope</code> ，并且如果节点中有多个指令，则只要其中一个指令是 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">true</code> 的设置，其它所有指令都会受影响。
</li>
</ul>

<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
这个参数还有其它取值。当其为 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">{}</code> 时，则 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">link</code> 接受一个完全隔离（isolate）的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope</code> ，于 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">true</code> 的区别就是不会继承其它 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope</code> 的属性。但是这时，这个 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope</code> 的属性却可以有很灵活的定义方式：
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
<span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">@attr</span> 引用节点的属性。
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;div ng-controller=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"TestCtrl"</span>&gt;
    &lt;div a abc=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"here"</span> xx=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"{{ a }}"</span> c=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"ccc"</span>&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
</pre></div>



<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> app <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> angular.module(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>, [], angular.noop);
  
  app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'a'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
    <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> func <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(element, attrs, link){
      <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(scope){
        console.log(scope);
      }
    }
  
    <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> func,
            scope<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> {a<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'@abc'</span>, b<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'@xx'</span>, c<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'@'</span>},
            restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'A'</span>};
  });
  
  app.controller(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'TestCtrl'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope){
    $scope.a <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'123'</span>;
  });
</pre></div>


<ul style="line-height: 1.4em; padding-left: 20px; margin: auto 30px;">
<li><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">@abc</span> 引用 div 节点的 abc 属性。
</li>
<li><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">@xx</span> 引用 div 节点的 xx 属性，而 xx 属性又是一个变量绑定，于是 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope</code> 中 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">b</code> 属性值就和 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">TestCtrl</code> 的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">a</code> 变量绑定在一起了。
</li>
<li><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">@</span> 没有写 attr name ，则默认取自己的值，这里是取 div 的 c 属性。
</li>
</ul>

<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
<span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">=attr</span> 相似，只是它把节点的属性值当成节点 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope</code> 的属性名来使用，作用相当于上面例子中的 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">@xx</span> ：
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;div ng-controller=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"TestCtrl"</span>&gt;
    &lt;div a abc=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"here"</span>&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
</pre></div>



<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> app <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> angular.module(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>, [], angular.noop);
  
  app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'a'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
    <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> func <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(element, attrs, link){
      <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(scope){
        console.log(scope);
      }
    }
  
    <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> func,
            scope<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> {a<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'=abc'</span>},
            restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'A'</span>};
  });
  
  app.controller(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'TestCtrl'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope){
    $scope.here <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'123'</span>;
  });
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
<span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">&amp;attr</span> 是包装一个函数出来，这个函数以节点所在的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope</code> 为上下文。来看一个很爽的例子：
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;div ng-controller=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"TestCtrl"</span>&gt;
    &lt;div a abc=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"here = here + 1"</span> ng-click=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"show(here)"</span>&gt;这里&lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;div&gt;{{ here }}&lt;/div&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
</pre></div>



<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"><span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 1</span>   <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> app <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> angular.module(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>, [], angular.noop);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 2</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 3</span>   app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'a'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 4</span>     <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> func <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(element, attrs, link){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 5</span>       <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span> llink(scope){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 6</span>         console.log(scope);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 7</span>         scope.a();
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 8</span>         scope.b();
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 9</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">10</span>         scope.show <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(here){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">11</span>           console.log(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Inner, '</span> <span style="color: #7fff00">+</span> here);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">12</span>           scope.a({here<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00ffff">5</span>});
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">13</span>         }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">14</span>       }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">15</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">16</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">17</span>     <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> func,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">18</span>             scope<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> {a<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'&amp;abc'</span>, b<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'&amp;ngClick'</span>},
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">19</span>             restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'A'</span>};
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">20</span>   });
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">21</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">22</span>   app.controller(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'TestCtrl'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">23</span>     $scope.here <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #00ffff">123</span>;
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">24</span>     console.log($scope);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">25</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">26</span>     $scope.show <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(here){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">27</span>       console.log(here);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">28</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">29</span>   });
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
scope.a 是 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">&amp;abc</span> ，即：
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  scope.a <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){here <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> here <span style="color: #7fff00">+</span> <span style="color: #00ffff">1</span>}
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
只是其中的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">here</code> 是 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">TestCtrl</code> 的。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
scope.b 是 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">&amp;ngClick</span> ，即：
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  scope.b <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){show(here)}
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
这里的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">show()</code> 和 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">here</code> 都是 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">TestCtrl</code> 的，于是上面的代码最开始会在终端输出一个 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">124</code> 。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
当点击“这里”时，这时执行的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">show(here)</code> 就是 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">llink</code> 中定义的那个函数了，与 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">TestCtrl</code> 无关。但是，其间的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope.a({here:5})</code> ，因为 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">a</code> 执行时是 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">TestCtrl</code> 的上下文，于是向 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">a</code> 传递的一个对象，里面的所有属性 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">TestCtrl</code> 就全收下了，接着执行 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">here=here+1</code> ，于是我们会在屏幕上看到 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">6</code> 。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
这里是一个上下文交错的环境，通过 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">&amp;</span> 这种机制，让指令的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope</code> 与节点的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope</code> 发生了互动。真是鬼斧神工的设计。而实现它，只用了几行代码：
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  <span style="color: #90ee90">case</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'&amp;'</span><span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> {
    parentGet <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> $parse(attrs[attrName]);
    scope[scopeName] <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(locals) {
      <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> parentGet(parentScope, locals);
    }
    <span style="color: #90ee90">break</span>;
  }
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
再看 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">controller</span> 这个参数。这个参数的作用是提供一个 controller 的构造函数，它会在 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">compile</code> 函数之后， <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">link</code> 函数之前被执行。
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;a&gt;haha&lt;/a&gt;
</pre></div>



<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"><span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 1</span>   <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> app <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> angular.module(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>, [], angular.noop);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 2</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 3</span>   app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'a'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 4</span>     <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> func <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 5</span>       console.log(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'compile'</span>);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 6</span>       <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 7</span>         console.log(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'link'</span>);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 8</span>       }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 9</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">10</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">11</span>     <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> controller <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope, $element, $attrs, $transclude){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">12</span>       console.log(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'controller'</span>);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">13</span>       console.log($scope);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">14</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">15</span>       <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> node <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> $transclude(<span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(clone_element, scope){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">16</span>         console.log(clone_element);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">17</span>         console.log(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'--'</span>);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">18</span>         console.log(scope);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">19</span>       });
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">20</span>       console.log(node);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">21</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">22</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">23</span>     <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> func,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">24</span>             controller<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> controller,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">25</span>             transclude<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #90ee90">true</span>,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">26</span>             restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'E'</span>}
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">27</span>   });
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
<code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">controller</code> 的最后一个参数， <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">$transclude</code> ，是一个只接受 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">cloneAttachFn</code> 作为参数的一个函数。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
按官方的说法，这个机制的设计目的是为了让各个指令之间可以互相通信。参考普通节点的处理方式，这里也是处理指令 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope</code> 的合适位置。
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;a b&gt;kk&lt;/a&gt;
</pre></div>



<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"><span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 1</span>   <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> app <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> angular.module(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>, [], angular.noop);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 2</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 3</span>   app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'a'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 4</span>     <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> func <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 5</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 6</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 7</span>     <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> controller <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope, $element, $attrs, $transclude){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 8</span>       console.log(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'a'</span>);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 9</span>       <span style="color: #90ee90">this</span>.a <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'xx'</span>;
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">10</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">11</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">12</span>     <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> func,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">13</span>             name<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'not_a'</span>,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">14</span>             controller<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> controller,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">15</span>             restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'E'</span>}
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">16</span>   });
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">17</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">18</span>   app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'b'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">19</span>     <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> func <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">20</span>       <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope, $element, $attrs, $controller){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">21</span>         console.log($controller);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">22</span>       }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">23</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">24</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">25</span>     <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> controller <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope, $element, $attrs, $transclude){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">26</span>       console.log(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'b'</span>);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">27</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">28</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">29</span>     <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> func,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">30</span>             controller<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> controller,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">31</span>             require<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'not_a'</span>,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">32</span>             restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'EA'</span>}
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">33</span>   });
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
<span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">name</span> 参数在这里可以用以为 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">controller</code> 重起一个名字，以方便在 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">require</span> 参数中引用。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
<span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">require</span> 参数可以带两种前缀（可以同时使用）：
</p>

<ul style="line-height: 1.4em; padding-left: 20px; margin: auto 30px;">
<li><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">?</span> ，如果指定的 controller 不存在，则忽略错误。即：
<p style="margin: 15px 0;"></p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  require<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'?not_b'</span>
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;"></p>
如果名为 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">not_b</code> 的 controller 不存在时，不会直接抛出错误， <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">link</code> 函数中对应的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">$controller</code> 为 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">undefined</code> 。
<p style="margin: 15px 0;"></p>
</li>
<li><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">^</span> ，同时在父级节点中寻找指定的 controller ，把上面的例子小改一下：
<p style="margin: 15px 0;"></p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;a&gt;&lt;b&gt;kk&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;"></p>
把 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">a</code> 的 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">require</span> 改成（否则就找不到 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">not_a</code> 这个 controller ）：
<p style="margin: 15px 0;"></p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  require: <span style="color: #00e5ee">'?^not_a'</span>
</pre></div>


</li>
</ul>

<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
还剩下几个模板参数：
</p>

<dl style="font-size: small; margin: 10px auto; padding: 10px; border-bottom: 1px dashed gray; border-top: 1px dashed gray;">
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">template</span> 模板内容，这个内容会根据 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">replace</span> 参数的设置替换节点或只替换节点内容。</dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
</dd>
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">templateUrl</span> 模板内容，获取方式是异步请求。</dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
</dd>
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">replace</span> 设置如何处理模板内容。为 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">true</code> 时为替换掉指令节点，否则只替换到节点内容。</dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
</dd>
</dl>


<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;div ng-controller=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"TestCtrl"</span>&gt;
    &lt;h1 a&gt;原始内容&lt;/h1&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
</pre></div>



<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> app <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> angular.module(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>, [], angular.noop);
  
  app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'a'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
    <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> func <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
    }
  
    <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> func,
            template<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'&lt;p&gt;标题 {{ name }} &lt;button ng-click="name=\'</span>hahaha\<span style="color: #00e5ee">'"&gt;修改&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/p&gt;'</span>,
            <span style="color: #507080">//replace: true,</span>
            <span style="color: #507080">//controller: function($scope){$scope.name = 'xxx'},</span>
            <span style="color: #507080">//scope: {},</span>
            scope<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #90ee90">true</span> ,
            controller<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope){console.log($scope)},
            restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'A'</span>}
  });
  
  app.controller(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'TestCtrl'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope){
    $scope.name <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'123'</span>;
    console.log($scope);
  });
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
<span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">template</span> 中可以包括变量引用的表达式，其 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope</code> 遵寻 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">scope</span> 参数的作用（可能受继承关系影响）。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
<span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">templateUrl</span> 是异步请求模板内容，并且是获取到内容之后才开始执行指令的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">compile</code> 函数。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
最后说一个 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">compile</span> 这个参数。它除了可以返回一个函数用为 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">link</code> 函数之外，还可以返回一个对象，这个对象能包括两个成员，一个 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">pre</span> ，一个 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">post</span> 。实际上， <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">link</code> 函数是由两部分组成，所谓的 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">preLink</span> 和 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">postLink</span> 。区别在于执行顺序，特别是在指令层级嵌套的结构之下， <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">postLink</span> 是在所有的子级指令 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">link</code> 完成之后才最后执行的。 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">compile</span> 如果只返回一个函数，则这个函数被作为 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">postLink</span> 使用：
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;a&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
</pre></div>



<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"><span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 1</span>   <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> app <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> angular.module(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>, [], angular.noop);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 2</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 3</span>   app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'a'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 4</span>     <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> func <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 5</span>       console.log(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'a compile'</span>);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 6</span>       <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 7</span>         pre<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){console.log(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'a link pre'</span>)},
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 8</span>         post<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){console.log(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'a link post'</span>)},
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 9</span>       }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">10</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">11</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">12</span>     <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> func,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">13</span>             restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'E'</span>}
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">14</span>   });
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">15</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">16</span>   app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'b'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">17</span>     <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> func <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">18</span>       console.log(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'b compile'</span>);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">19</span>       <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">20</span>         pre<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){console.log(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'b link pre'</span>)},
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">21</span>         post<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){console.log(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'b link post'</span>)},
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">22</span>       }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">23</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">24</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">25</span>     <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> func,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">26</span>             restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'E'</span>}
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">27</span>   });
</pre></div>


<a name="toc77"></a>
<h2 style=" border-bottom: 1px solid #69ab01; color: #5e9802; padding: 2px; text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px gray; margin: 20px auto; font-size: medium;">18.9. Attributes的细节</h2>

<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
节点属性被包装之后会传给 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">compile</code> 和 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">link</code> 函数。从这个操作中，我们可以得到节点的引用，可以操作节点属性，也可以为节点属性注册侦听事件。
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;test a=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"1"</span> b c=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"xxx"</span>&gt;&lt;/test&gt;
</pre></div>



<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> app <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> angular.module(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>, [], angular.noop);
  
  app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'test'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
    <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> func <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($element, $attrs){
      console.log($attrs);
    }
  
    <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> func,
            restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'E'</span>}
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
整个 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">Attributes</span> 对象是比较简单的，它的成员包括了：
</p>

<dl style="font-size: small; margin: 10px auto; padding: 10px; border-bottom: 1px dashed gray; border-top: 1px dashed gray;">
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$$element</span> 属性所在的节点。</dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
</dd>
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$attr</span> 所有的属性值（类型是对象）。</dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
</dd>
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$normalize</span> 一个名字标准化的工具函数，可以把 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">ng-click</code> 变成 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">ngClick</code> 。</dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
</dd>
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$observe</span> 为属性注册侦听器的函数。</dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
</dd>
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$set</span> 设置对象属性，及节点属性的工具。</dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
</dd>
</dl>

<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
除了上面这些成员，对象的成员还包括所有属性的名字。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
先看 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$observe</span> 的使用，基本上相当于 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$scope</span> 中的 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$watch</span> ：
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;div ng-controller=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"TestCtrl"</span>&gt;
    &lt;test a=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"{{ a }}"</span> b c=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"xxx"</span>&gt;&lt;/test&gt;
    &lt;button ng-click=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"a=a+1"</span>&gt;修改&lt;/button&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
</pre></div>



<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> app <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> angular.module(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>, [], angular.noop);
  
  app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'test'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
    <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> func <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($element, $attrs){
      console.log($attrs);
  
      $attrs.$observe(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'a'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(new_v){
        console.log(new_v);
      });
    }
  
    <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> func,
            restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'E'</span>}
  });
  
  app.controller(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'TestCtrl'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope){
    $scope.a <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #00ffff">123</span>;
  });
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
<span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$set</span> 方法的定义是： <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">function(key, value, writeAttr, attrName) { ... }</code> 。
</p>

<ul style="line-height: 1.4em; padding-left: 20px; margin: auto 30px;">
<li><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">key</span> 对象的成员名。
</li>
<li><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">value</span> 需要设置的值。
</li>
<li><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">writeAttr</span> 是否同时修改 DOM 节点的属性（注意区别“节点”与“对象”），默认为 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">true</code> 。
</li>
<li><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">attrName</span> 实际的属性名，与“标准化”之后的属性名有区别。
</li>
</ul>


<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;div ng-controller=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"TestCtrl"</span>&gt;
    &lt;test a=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"1"</span> ys-a=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"123"</span> ng-click=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"show(1)"</span>&gt;这里&lt;/test&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
</pre></div>



<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> app <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> angular.module(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>, [], angular.noop);
  
  app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'test'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
    <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> func <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($element, $attrs){
      $attrs.$set(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'b'</span>, <span style="color: #00e5ee">'ooo'</span>);
      $attrs.$set(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'a-b'</span>, <span style="color: #00e5ee">'11'</span>);
      $attrs.$set(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'c-d'</span>, <span style="color: #00e5ee">'11'</span>, <span style="color: #90ee90">true</span>, <span style="color: #00e5ee">'c_d'</span>);
      console.log($attrs);
    }
  
    <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> func,
            restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'E'</span>}
  });
  
  app.controller(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'TestCtrl'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope){
    $scope.show <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(v){console.log(v);}
  });
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
从例子中可以看到，原始的节点属性值对，放到对象中之后，名字一定是“标准化”之后的。但是手动 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">$set</code> 的新属性，不会自动做标准化处理。
</p>

<a name="toc78"></a>
<h2 style=" border-bottom: 1px solid #69ab01; color: #5e9802; padding: 2px; text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px gray; margin: 20px auto; font-size: medium;">18.10. 预定义的 NgModelController</h2>

<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
在前面讲 conroller 参数的时候，提到过可以为指令定义一个 conroller 。官方的实现中，有很多已定义的指令，这些指令当中，有两个已定义的 conroller ，它们是 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">NgModelController</span> 和 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">FormController</span> ，对应 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">ng-model</span> 和 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">form</span> 这两个指令（可以参照前面的“表单控件”一章）。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
在使用中，除了可以通过 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">$scope</code> 来取得它们的引用之外，也可以在自定义指令中通过 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">require</span> 参数直接引用，这样就可以在 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">link</code> 函数中使用 controller 去实现一些功能。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
先看 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">NgModelController</span> 。这东西的作用有两个，一是控制 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">ViewValue</code> 与 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">ModelValue</code> 之间的转换关系（你可以实现看到的是一个值，但是存到变量里变成了另外一个值），二是与 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">FormController</span> 配合做数据校验的相关逻辑。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
先看两个应该是最有用的属性：
</p>

<dl style="font-size: small; margin: 10px auto; padding: 10px; border-bottom: 1px dashed gray; border-top: 1px dashed gray;">
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$formatters</span> 是一个由函数组成的列表，串行执行，作用是把变量值变成显示的值。</dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
</dd>
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$parsers</span> 与上面的方向相反，把显示的值变成变量值。</dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
</dd>
</dl>

<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
假设我们在变量中要保存一个列表的类型，但是显示的东西只能是字符串，所以这两者之间需要一个转换：
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;div ng-controller=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"TestCtrl"</span>&gt;
    &lt;input type=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"text"</span> ng-model=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"a"</span> test /&gt;
    &lt;button ng-click=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"show(a)"</span>&gt;查看&lt;/button&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
</pre></div>



<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"><span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 1</span>   <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> app <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> angular.module(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>, [], angular.noop);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 2</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 3</span>   app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'test'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 4</span>     <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> link <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope, $element, $attrs, $ctrl){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 5</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 6</span>       $ctrl.$formatters.push(<span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(value){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 7</span>         <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> value.join(<span style="color: #00e5ee">','</span>);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 8</span>       });
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 9</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">10</span>       $ctrl.$parsers.push(<span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(value){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">11</span>         <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> value.split(<span style="color: #00e5ee">','</span>);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">12</span>       });
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">13</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">14</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">15</span>     <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){<span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> link},
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">16</span>             require<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'ngModel'</span>,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">17</span>             restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'A'</span>}
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">18</span>   });
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">19</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">20</span>   app.controller(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'TestCtrl'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">21</span>     $scope.a <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> [];
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">22</span>     <span style="color: #507080">//$scope.a = [1,2,3];</span>
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">23</span>     $scope.show <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(v){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">24</span>       console.log(v);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">25</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">26</span>   });
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
上面在定义 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">test</code> 这个指令， <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">require</span> 参数指定了 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">ngModel</code> 。同时因为 DOM 结构， <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">ng-model</code> 是存在的。于是， <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">link</code> 函数中就可以获取到一个 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">NgModelController</span> 的实例，即代码中的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">$ctrl</code> 。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
我们添加了需要的过滤函数：
</p>

<ul style="line-height: 1.4em; padding-left: 20px; margin: auto 30px;">
<li>从变量( <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">ModelValue</code> )到显示值( <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">ViewValue</code> )的过程， <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">$formatters</code> 属性，把一个列表变成一个字符串。
</li>
<li>从显示值到变量的过程， <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">$parsers</code> 属性，把一个字符串变成一个列表。
</li>
</ul>

<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
对于显示值和变量，还有其它的 API ，这里就不细说了。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
另一部分，是关于数据校验的，放到下一章同 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">FormController</span> 一起讨论。
</p>

<a name="toc79"></a>
<h2 style=" border-bottom: 1px solid #69ab01; color: #5e9802; padding: 2px; text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px gray; margin: 20px auto; font-size: medium;">18.11. 预定义的 FormController</h2>

<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
前面的“表单控制”那章，实际上讲的就是 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">FormController</span> ，只是那里是从 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope</code> 中获取到的引用。现在从指令定义的角度，来更清楚地了解 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">FormController</span> 及 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">NgModelController</span> 是如何配合工作的。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
先说一下， <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">form</span> 和 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">ngForm</span> 是官方定义的两个指令，但是它们其实是同一个东西。前者只允许以标签形式使用，而后者允许 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">EAC</code> 的形式。DOM 结构中， <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">form</code> 标签不能嵌套，但是 ng 的指令没有这个限制。不管是 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">form</span> 还是 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">ngForm</span> ，它们的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">controller</code> 都被命名成了 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">form</code> 。 所以 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">require</span> 这个参数不要写错了。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
<span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">FormController</span> 的几个成员是很好理解的：
</p>

<dl style="font-size: small; margin: 10px auto; padding: 10px; border-bottom: 1px dashed gray; border-top: 1px dashed gray;">
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$pristine</span> 表单是否被动过</dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
</dd>
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$dirty</span> 表单是否没被动过</dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
</dd>
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$valid</span> 表单是否检验通过</dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
</dd>
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$invalid</span> 表单是否检验未通过</dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
</dd>
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$error</span> 表单中的错误</dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
</dd>
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$setDirty()</span> 直接设置 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$dirty</span> 及 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$pristine</span> </dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
</dd>
</dl>


<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;div ng-controller=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"TestCtrl"</span>&gt;
    &lt;div ng-form test&gt;
      &lt;input ng-model=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"a"</span> type=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"email"</span> /&gt;
      &lt;button ng-click=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"do()"</span>&gt;查看&lt;/button&gt;
    &lt;/div&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
</pre></div>



<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> app <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> angular.module(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>, [], angular.noop);
  
  app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'test'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
    <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> link <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope, $element, $attrs, $ctrl){
      $scope.<span style="color: #90ee90">do</span> <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
        <span style="color: #507080">//$ctrl.$setDirty();</span>
        console.log($ctrl.$pristine); <span style="color: #507080">//form是否没被动过</span>
        console.log($ctrl.$dirty); <span style="color: #507080">//form是否被动过</span>
        console.log($ctrl.$valid); <span style="color: #507080">//form是否被检验通过</span>
        console.log($ctrl.$invalid); <span style="color: #507080">//form是否有错误</span>
        console.log($ctrl.$error); <span style="color: #507080">//form中有错误的字段</span>
      }
    }
  
    <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){<span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> link},
            require<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'form'</span>,
            restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'A'</span>}
  });
  
  app.controller(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'TestCtrl'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope){
  });
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
<span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$error</span> 这个属性，是一个对象， <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">key</code> 是错误名， <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">value</code> 部分是一个列表，其成员是对应的 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">NgModelController</span> 的实例。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
<span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">FormController</span> 可以自由增减它包含的那些，类似于 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">NgModelController</span> 的实例。在 DOM 结构上，有 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">ng-model</code> 的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">input</code> 节点的 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">NgMoelController</span> 会被自动添加。
</p>

<dl style="font-size: small; margin: 10px auto; padding: 10px; border-bottom: 1px dashed gray; border-top: 1px dashed gray;">
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$addControl()</span> 添加一个 conroller </dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
</dd>
<dt style="border-left: 4px solid rgb(215, 81, 0); padding-left: 5px; margin: 5px auto;"><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$removeControl()</span> 删除一个 controller</dt><dd style="margin-left: 30px;">
</dd>
</dl>

<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
这两个手动使用机会应该不会很多。被添加的实例也可以手动实现所有的 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">NgModelController</span> 的方法
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;div ng-controller=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"TestCtrl"</span>&gt;
    &lt;bb /&gt;
    &lt;div ng-form test&gt;
      &lt;input ng-model=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"a"</span> type=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"email"</span> /&gt;
      &lt;button ng-click=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"add()"</span>&gt;添加&lt;/button&gt;
    &lt;/div&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
</pre></div>



<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"><span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 1</span>   <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> app <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> angular.module(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>, [], angular.noop);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 2</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 3</span>   app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'test'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 4</span>     <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> link <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope, $element, $attrs, $ctrl){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 5</span>       $scope.add <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 6</span>         $ctrl.$addControl($scope.bb);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 7</span>         console.log($ctrl);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 8</span>       }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 9</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">10</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">11</span>     <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){<span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> link},
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">12</span>             require<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'form'</span>,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">13</span>             restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'A'</span>}
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">14</span>   });
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">15</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">16</span>   app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'bb'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">17</span>     <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> controller <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope, $element, $attrs, $transclude){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">18</span>       $scope.bb <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #90ee90">this</span>;
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">19</span>       <span style="color: #90ee90">this</span>.$name <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'bb'</span>;
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">20</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">21</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">22</span>     <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> angular.noop,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">23</span>             restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'E'</span>,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">24</span>             controller<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> controller}
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">25</span>   });
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">26</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">27</span>   app.controller(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'TestCtrl'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">28</span>   });
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
整合 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">FormController</span> 和 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">NgModelController</span> 就很容易扩展各种类型的字段:
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;div ng-controller=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"TestCtrl"</span>&gt;
    &lt;form name=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"f"</span>&gt;
      &lt;input type=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"my"</span> ng-model=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"a"</span> /&gt;
      &lt;button ng-click=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"show()"</span>&gt;查看&lt;/button&gt;
    &lt;/form&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
</pre></div>



<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"><span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 1</span>   var app = angular.module('Demo', [], angular.noop);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 2</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 3</span>   app.directive('input', function(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 4</span>     var link = function($scope, $element, $attrs, $ctrl){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 5</span>       console.log($attrs.type);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 6</span>       var validator = function(v){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 7</span>         if(v == '123'){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 8</span>           $ctrl.$setValidity('my', true);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 9</span>           return v;
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">10</span>         } else {
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">11</span>           $ctrl.$setValidity('my', false);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">12</span>           return undefined;
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">13</span>         }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">14</span>       }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">15</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">16</span>       $ctrl.$formatters.push(validator);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">17</span>       $ctrl.$parsers.push(validator);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">18</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">19</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">20</span>     return {compile: function(){return link},
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">21</span>             require: 'ngModel',
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">22</span>             restrict: 'E'}
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">23</span>   });
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">24</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">25</span>   app.controller('TestCtrl', function($scope){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">26</span>       $scope.show = function(){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">27</span>         console.log($scope.f);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">28</span>       }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">29</span>   });
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
虽然官方原来定义了几种 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">type</code> ，但这不妨碍我们继续扩展新的类型。如果新的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">type</code> 参数值不在官方的定义列表里，那会按 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">text</code> 类型先做处理，这其实什么影响都没有。剩下的，就是写我们自己的验证逻辑就行了。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
上面的代码是参见官方的做法，使用格式化的过程，同时在里面做有效性检查。
</p>

<a name="toc80"></a>
<h2 style=" border-bottom: 1px solid #69ab01; color: #5e9802; padding: 2px; text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px gray; margin: 20px auto; font-size: medium;">18.12. 示例：文本框</h2>

<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
这个例子与官网上的那个例子相似。最终是要显示一个文本框，这个文本框由标题和内容两部分组成。而且标题和内容则是引用 controller 中的变量值。
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
HTML 部分的代码：
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;div ng-controller=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"TestCtrl"</span>&gt;
    &lt;ys-block title=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"title"</span> text=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"text"</span>&gt;&lt;/ys-block&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;标题: &lt;input ng-model=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"title"</span> /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;内容: &lt;input ng-model=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"text"</span> /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
    &lt;ys-block title=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"title"</span> text=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"text"</span>&gt;&lt;/ys-block&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
从这个期望实现效果的 HTML 代码中，我们可以考虑设计指令的实现方式：
</p>

<ul style="line-height: 1.4em; padding-left: 20px; margin: auto 30px;">
<li>这个指令的使用方式是“标签”， 即 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">restrict</span> 这个参数应该设置为 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">E</code> 。
</li>
<li>节点的属性值是对 controller 变量的引用，那么我们应该在指令的 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">scope</span> 中使用 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">=</code> 的方式来指定成员值。
</li>
<li>最终的效果显示需要进行 DOM 结构的重构，那直接使用 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">template</span> 就好了。
</li>
<li>自定义的标签在最终效果中是多余的，所有 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">replace</span> 应该设置为 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">true</code> 。
</li>
</ul>

<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
JS 部分的代码：
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> app <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> angular.module(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>, [], angular.noop);
  
  app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'ysBlock'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(){
    <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> angular.noop,
            template<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'&lt;div style="width: 200px; border: 1px solid black;"&gt;&lt;h1 style="background-color: gray; color: white; font-size: 22px;"&gt;{{ title }}&lt;/h1&gt;&lt;div&gt;{{ text }}&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;'</span>,
            replace<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #90ee90">true</span>,
            scope<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> {title<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'=title'</span>, text<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'=text'</span>},
            restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'E'</span>};
  });
  
  app.controller(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'TestCtrl'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope){
    $scope.title <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'标题在这里'</span>;
    $scope.text <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'内容在这里'</span>;
  });
  
  angular.bootstrap(document, [<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>]);
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
可以看到，这种简单的组件式指令，只需要作 DOM 结构的变换即可实现，连 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">compile</code> 函数都不需要写。
</p>

<a name="toc81"></a>
<h2 style=" border-bottom: 1px solid #69ab01; color: #5e9802; padding: 2px; text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px gray; margin: 20px auto; font-size: medium;">18.13. 示例：模板控制语句 for</h2>

<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
这个示例尝试实现一个重复语句，功能同官方的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">ngRepeat</code> ，但是使用方式类似于我们通常编程语言中的 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">for</span> 语句：
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;div ng-controller=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"TestCtrl"</span> ng-init=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"obj_list=[1,2,3,4]; name='name'"</span>&gt;
    &lt;ul&gt;
      &lt;for o in obj_list&gt;
        &lt;li&gt;{{ o }}, {{ name }}&lt;/li&gt;
      &lt;/for&gt;
    &lt;/ul&gt;
    &lt;button ng-click=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"obj_list=[1,2]; name='o?'"</span>&gt;修改&lt;/button&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
同样，我们从上面的使用方式去考虑这个指令的实现：
</p>

<ul style="line-height: 1.4em; padding-left: 20px; margin: auto 30px;">
<li>这是一个完全的控制指令，所以单个节点应该只有它一个指令起作用就好了，于是权重要比较高，并且“到此为止”—— <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">priority</span> 设置为 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">1000</code> ， <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">terminal</span> 设置为 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">true</code> 。
</li>
<li>使用时的语法问题。事实上浏览器会把 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">for</code> 节点补充成一个正确的 HTML 结构，即里面的属性都会变成类似 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">o=""</code> 这样。我们通过节点的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">outerHTML</code> 属性取到字符串并解析取得需要的信息。
</li>
<li>我们把 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">for</code> 节点之间的内容作为一个模板，并且通过循环多次渲染该模板之后把结果填充到合适的位置。
</li>
