<li>在处理上面的那个模板时，需要不断地创建新 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope</code> 的，并且 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">o</code> 这个成员需要单独赋值。
</li>
</ul>

<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
注意：这里只是简单实现功能。官方的那个 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">ngRepeat</span> 比较复杂，是做了专门的算法优化的。当然，这里的实现也可以是简单把 DOM 结构变成使用 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">ngRepeat</span> 的形式 :)
</p>
<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
JS 部分代码：
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"><span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 1</span>   <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> app <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> angular.module(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>, [], angular.noop);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 2</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 3</span>   app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'for'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($compile){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 4</span>     <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> compile <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($element, $attrs, $link){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 5</span>       <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> match <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> $element[<span style="color: #00ffff">0</span>].outerHTML.match(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'&lt;for (.*?)=.*? in=.*? (.*?)=.*?&gt;'</span>);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 6</span>       <span style="color: #90ee90">if</span>(<span style="color: #7fff00">!</span>match <span style="color: #7fff00">||</span> match.length <span style="color: #7fff00">!=</span> <span style="color: #00ffff">3</span>){<span style="color: #90ee90">throw</span> Error(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'syntax: &lt;for o in obj_list&gt;'</span>)}
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 7</span>       <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> iter <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> match[<span style="color: #00ffff">1</span>];
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 8</span>       <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> list <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> match[<span style="color: #00ffff">2</span>];
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 9</span>       <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> tpl <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> $compile($.trim($element.html()));
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">10</span>       $element.empty();
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">11</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">12</span>       <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> link <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope, $ielement, $iattrs, $controller){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">13</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">14</span>         <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> new_node <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> [];
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">15</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">16</span>         $scope.$watch(list, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(list){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">17</span>           angular.forEach(new_node, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(n){n.remove()});
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">18</span>           <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> scp, inode;
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">19</span>           <span style="color: #90ee90">for</span>(<span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> i <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #00ffff">0</span>, ii <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> list.length; i <span style="color: #7fff00">&lt;</span> ii; i<span style="color: #7fff00">++</span>){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">20</span>             scp <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> $scope.$new();
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">21</span>             scp[iter] <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> list[i];
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">22</span>             inode <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> tpl(scp, angular.noop);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">23</span>             $ielement.before(inode);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">24</span>             new_node.push(inode);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">25</span>           }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">26</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">27</span>         });
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">28</span>       }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">29</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">30</span>       <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> link;
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">31</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">32</span>     <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> compile,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">33</span>             priority<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00ffff">1000</span>,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">34</span>             terminal<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #90ee90">true</span>,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">35</span>             restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'E'</span>};
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">36</span>   });
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">37</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">38</span>   app.controller(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'TestCtrl'</span>, angular.noop);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">39</span>   angular.bootstrap(document, [<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>]);
</pre></div>


<a name="toc82"></a>
<h2 style=" border-bottom: 1px solid #69ab01; color: #5e9802; padding: 2px; text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px gray; margin: 20px auto; font-size: medium;">18.14. 示例：模板控制语句 if/else</h2>

<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
这个示例是尝试实现：
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;">  &lt;div ng-controller=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"TestCtrl"</span>&gt;
    &lt;if true=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"a == 1"</span>&gt;
        &lt;p&gt;判断为真, {{ name }}&lt;/p&gt;
      &lt;else&gt;
        &lt;p&gt;判断为假, {{ name }}&lt;/p&gt;
      &lt;/else&gt;
    &lt;/if&gt;
  
    &lt;div&gt;
      &lt;p&gt;a: &lt;input ng-model=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"a"</span> /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
      &lt;p&gt;name: &lt;input ng-model=<span style="color: #00e5ee">"name"</span> /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
    &lt;/div&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
考虑实现的思路：
</p>

<ul style="line-height: 1.4em; padding-left: 20px; margin: auto 30px;">
<li><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">else</span> 与 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">if</span> 是两个指令，它们是父子关系。通过 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope</code> 可以联系起来。至于 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">scope</code> 是在 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">link</code> 中处理还是 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">controller</code> 中处理并不重要。
</li>
<li><span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">true</span> 属性的条件判断通过 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">$parse</span> 服务很容易实现。
</li>
<li>如果最终效果要去掉 <span style="color: rgb(215, 81, 0);">if</span> 节点，我们可以使用注释节点来“占位”。
</li>
</ul>

<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
JS 代码：
</p>

<div style="background: #103040"><pre style="white-space: pre-wrap; word-wrap: break-word; border: 1px solid rgb(136, 136, 136); font-size: small; line-height: 1.5em; padding: 5px; color: rgb(224, 238, 224); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"><span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 1</span>   <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> app <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> angular.module(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>, [], angular.noop);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 2</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 3</span>   app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'if'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($parse, $compile){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 4</span>     <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> compile <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($element, $attrs){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 5</span>       <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> cond <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> $parse($attrs.<span style="color: #90ee90">true</span>);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 6</span>       
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 7</span>       <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> link <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope, $ielement, $iattrs, $controller){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 8</span>         $scope.if_node <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> $compile($.trim($ielement.html()))($scope, angular.noop);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px"> 9</span>         $ielement.empty();
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">10</span>         <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> mark <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> $(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'&lt;!-- IF/ELSE --&gt;'</span>);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">11</span>         $element.before(mark);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">12</span>         $element.remove();
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">13</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">14</span>         $scope.$watch(<span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>(scope){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">15</span>           <span style="color: #90ee90">if</span>(cond(scope)){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">16</span>             mark.after($scope.if_node);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">17</span>             $scope.else_node.detach();
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">18</span>           } <span style="color: #90ee90">else</span> {
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">19</span>             <span style="color: #90ee90">if</span>($scope.else_node <span style="color: #7fff00">!==</span> <span style="color: #90ee90">undefined</span>){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">20</span>               mark.after($scope.else_node);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">21</span>               $scope.if_node.detach();
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">22</span>             }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">23</span>           }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">24</span>         });
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">25</span>       }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">26</span>       <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> link;
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">27</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">28</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">29</span>     <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> compile,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">30</span>             scope<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #90ee90">true</span>,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">31</span>             restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'E'</span>}
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">32</span>   });
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">33</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">34</span>   app.directive(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'else'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($compile){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">35</span>     <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> compile <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($element, $attrs){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">36</span>       
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">37</span>       <span style="color: #bcd2ee">var</span> link <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope, $ielement, $iattrs, $controller){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">38</span>         $scope.else_node <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> $compile($.trim($ielement.html()))($scope, angular.noop);
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">39</span>         $element.remove();
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">40</span>       }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">41</span>       <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> link;
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">42</span>     }
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">43</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">44</span>     <span style="color: #90ee90">return</span> {compile<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> compile,
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">45</span>             restrict<span style="color: #7fff00">:</span> <span style="color: #00e5ee">'E'</span>}
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">46</span>   });
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">47</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">48</span>   app.controller(<span style="color: #00e5ee">'TestCtrl'</span>, <span style="color: #bcd2ee">function</span>($scope){
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">49</span>     $scope.a <span style="color: #7fff00">=</span> <span style="color: #00ffff">1</span>;
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">50</span>   });
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">51</span>   
<span style="color: gray; padding: 0 5px 0 5px">52</span>   angular.bootstrap(document, [<span style="color: #00e5ee">'Demo'</span>]);
</pre></div>


<p style="margin: 15px 0;">
代码中注意一点，就是 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">if_node</code> 在得到之时，就已经是做了变量绑定的了。错误的思路是，在 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">$watch</code> 中再去不断地得到新的 <code style="margin: auto 3px; color: rgb(34, 139, 34);">if_node</code> 。</p>
                                                                                        </td>
                                                                                    </tr>
                                                                                </tbody>
                                                                            </table>
